 dengue kaa virus desh ke mahanagaron main prakope failaata ja rahaa he
 In such a situation, it is important to know what to do to avoid it
 1
 Usually dengue mosquito bites during the day
 isliye din main machharon ke kaatane se khud ko bachaaen
 2
 barish ke dinon main phul shart hi pahanen
 Must wear shoes in feet
 sharir ko kahin se bhi khulaa naa choden
 3
 ghar ke aasapaas yaa ghar ke andar pani nahin jamane den
 Immediately drain frozen water in coolers, pottery, tires, etc
 4
 If there is water in the cooler, add kerosene oil to it so that the mosquito does not flourish
 5
 Use a mosquito net and remove the pimples
 6
 Cover the water tanks properly
 7
 If you have dengue, then keep avoiding these so that your body's virus does not reach others
 8
 First get help from the nearest doctor and get the platelets examined in the blood
 9
 The main method of treatment is to provide adjuvant therapy
 rogi ko lagaataar pani dete rahen nahin to sharir main pani kii kami ho sakati he
 Fluid is also given to the patient through the veins
 10
 Blood transfusion may also occur if the number of platelets in the patient's blood is too low or if the bleeding starts
 11
 Do not take any medicine by yourself because bleeding can increase if you accidentally took aspirin or any other non-steroidal drugs
 12
 There is no harm in giving ordinary paracetamol to the patient
